# Mission & Bounty Drop Tables
FORMAT: Mission rewards organized by ## Planet, ### Node — Mode. Rotation rewards in tables: Item | Rarity | Chance. Bounties show tier rewards with stage and % in tables.
INDEX: Mission Rewards (24 entries) | Sortie Rewards (1 entries) | Transient Rewards (51 entries) | Key Rewards (24 entries) | Cetus Bounty Rewards (10 entries) | Solaris Bounty Rewards (11 entries) | Deimos Bounty Rewards (12 entries) | Zariman Bounty Rewards (5 entries) | Entrati Lab Rewards (5 entries) | Hex Bounty Rewards (7 entries)
